 ) The incidents of mob lynching in India are not taking the name of freeze
 bheed dwaara kanoon ko haath main lene or ugr hokar kisi maamle ke aaropee kii peet-petakar hatya karnaa behad chintajanak he
 Now the latest case is in Rajsamand district of Rajasthan, where head constable Abdul Ghani, who went to investigate a land dispute in Bhima subdivision, was beaten to death by a mob
 desh kii sabase badi adaalat bhi mob linching kii ghatnaon ko lekar behad sakht he
 During the hearing of the Tehsin Poonawala case, the Supreme Court has even issued guidelines for the central government and state governments to prevent incidents of mob lynching
 is dauraan supreme court ne kaha tha ki har naagarik ke jivan kii raksha karnaa sarkaar kaa kartavya he
 Article 21 of the constitution gives every citizen the right to life and no life can be taken away without the procedure established by law
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki agar kisi ne aparaadh kiya he to usko kanoon ke daayre main laakar hi sajaa di jaaegi
 Only the court can punish if a person is accused in a case, then only the court can convict and punish him by following the judicial process
 adaalat ke sivaay kisi anya vyakti yaa sanstha yaa samooh ko kisi aparaadh ke aaropee vyakti ko doshi tehraane or sajaa dene kaa adhikaar nahin he
 If any person, group or organization does this, it is a crime, for which they will have to face punishment
 kai baar dekha jaataa he ki kisi maamle kaa aaropee bizzat bari ho jaataa he
 In such a situation, it is lawfully unfair to call an accused a criminal
 nyaay kii avadharana he ki jab tak kisi vyakti ko kisi aparaadh ke liye doshi nahin tehra diya jaataa he, tab tak usko nirdosh hi samajha jayega
 Only the rule of law will run in Hindustan
 Apart from this, in the Krishnamurthy v
 Shivkumar case, the Supreme Court made a strong comment about mobilization, saying that in a civilized society, only the rule of law prevails and the law is supreme
 bheed yaa koi group kanoon haath main lekar kisi aparaadh ke aaropee ko sajaa nahin de sakati he
 According to Advocate Markandeya Pant, at present, in the case of mob lynching, the police is the first to register a case under Section 153 a of the Indian Penal Code
 isamen 3 saal tak kii sajaa or jurmaane kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 Apart from this, action can be taken under sections 34, 147, 148 and 149 of IPC
 unka kahana he ki agar bheed dwaara kisi kii peet-petakar hatya kar di jaati he, to ipisi ki dhara 302 ke tahat mukadmaa darj kiya jayega or saath main dhara 34 yaa 149 lagaai jaaegi
 After this, all those who have been involved in mob lynching will be convicted of murder and punished by hanging or life imprisonment
 iske alaava sabhi par jurmaana bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Markandeya Pant says that if any person of the mob commits any crime, then everyone involved in the mob will be guilty for that crime
 saath hi sabhi ko us aparaadh ke liye alag-alag sajaa bhogani hogi
 What is the Supreme Court's Guidelines on Mob lynching During the Tehsin Poonawala case hearing in 2018, the Supreme Court issued a guideline to stop mob lynching
 ye guideline centre sarkaar or sabhi rajya sarkaron ke liye jari kii gai he
 Let us know what is the guideline of the Supreme Court
 
 
 
 
 1
 The Supreme Court said that all state governments should appoint a nodal officer in each district, who should be an officer of the rank of Superintendent of Police (SP) or above, to prevent incidents of mob violence and mob lynching
 is nodel adhikari ke saath dspi rank ke ek adhikari ko bhi tainaat kiya janaa chahie
 These officers will form a Special Task Force to stop the mobs lynching in the district, which will gather information and take action against those involved in such crimes, making inflammatory statements and spreading fake news through social media
 2
 The areas where mob lynching occurred during the last five years should be identified and its report prepared within three weeks of the order's issuance
 3
 The Home Secretaries of all the states should issue instructions to the police station in-charge and nodal officers for extra vigilance in areas where mob lynching has been reported
 4
 Nodal officers should meet regularly with local intelligence units and shos to take steps to prevent such incidents
 saath jis samudaay yaa jati ko mob linching kaa shikaar banaae jane kii ashanka ho, uske khilaaf bigade maahaul ko thik karne kii koshish kii jaae
 5
 rajyon ke dijipi or grih vibhaag ke sachiv jilon ke nodel adhikariyon or police intelegence ke pramukhon ke saath niyamit rup se baithak karen
 If steps can be taken to stop the problems of coordination between any two districts
 6
 Police officers try to disperse the mob using the powers given in Section 129 of the Criminal Procedure Code (CRPC)
 7
 The Union Home Department should also take initiative to coordinate between the state governments to prevent incidents of mob lynching
 8
 Central government and state governments should try to tell people through radio, television and media or through website that if someone tries to break the law and get involved in mob lynching, strict action will be taken against the law
 9
 It is the responsibility of the central government and the state governments to take steps to remove all objectionable content, including rumor-mongering posts and videos from social media, to prevent such incidents
 10
 To file or instigate the police for mob lynching, file an FIR and take action against those who spread the message or video under Section 153A of IPC and other relevant laws
 11
 In this regard, the central government should issue instructions to all state governments
 mob linching hone par fouran ho karrwai12
 If, despite all efforts, incidents of mob lynching occur, the police stations of the concerned area should immediately file an FIR without any hijabali
 13
 After registering the FIR for the incident of mob lynching, the concerned police station in-charge should immediately inform the Nodal Officer
 iske baad nodel adhikari kii duty hogi ki wo maamle kii jaanch kare or peedit parivaar ke khilaaf aage kii kisi bhi hinsa ko rokane ke liye kadam uthaae
 14
 nodel adhikari ko sunishchit karnaa hoga ki mob linching kii ghatnaon kii prabhavi jaanch ho or samay par maamle kii chargeshit daakhil kii ja sake
 Government made a scheme to give compensation to the victims 15
 rajya sarkaar aisi yojana taiyaar karen, jisase mob linching ke shikaar logon ko siarpisi kii dhara 357A ke tahat muaavja dene kii vyavastha kii jaae
 Case hearing to be completed in 6 months 16
 aise maamalon kii sunwaayee ke liye har jile main fast trek court banaai jaaen, jahaan par aise maamalon kii sunwaayee rojaanaa ho sake or trial 6 maheene ke andar puraa ho sake
 Listen to the victims before giving bail to the accused of mob lynching
 mob linching ke aropiyon ko jamaanat dene, parole dene yaa phir reeha karne ke maamle main vichaar karne se pehle court peedit parivaar kii bhi baat sune
 For this, they should be called by issuing notice
 18
 Families of mob lynching should be provided free legal aid
 iske liye unako legal sarvice athurity act 1987 ke tahat free main edwocket uplabdh karana chahie
 19
 agar koi adhikari apni duty nibhaane main vifal rahata he yaa phir maamle main samay par chargeshit file nahin karata he, to uske khilaaf departmental ection liya janaa chahie
 The UP Law Panel recommended the death sentence, the Uttar Pradesh Law Commission has recommended the death penalty to those accused of mob lynching
 upi lau kamishan ne uttar pradesh combating of mob linching act kaa masauda bhi pesh kiya he
 It also said that the responsibility of the police officer of that area should also be fixed
 agar usko duty main laaparvaahee karne kaa doshi paaya jaae to uske khilaaf hi dandatmak karrwai kii jaae

 jawaab main pune ne aakhri gend par dhoni ke chamatkaarik chakke kii badaulat chah wicket par 173 ran bana daale
 His defeat seemed certain at a time when he needed 23 runs in the last over

 is gend par dhoni or ravichandran aswin ne koi ran nahin liya
 On the next two balls, Dhoni hit a four and a six, but even then his team needed six runs on the last ball
 patel kii phullangth gend par dhoni ne midwicket ke upar chakka lagaakar sabit kar diya ki unki ginati duniya ke sarvshereshth match finishron main kyon hoti he or unka boria-bistar bandhawa chuke aalochakon ko bhi jawaab de diya
 After this win, Pune, who were among the two new teams of the IPL, survived the last place
 usne 14 maichon main paanch jeet or nau haar ke saath 10 ank lekar saatvaan sthaan hasil kiya, jabaki punjab 14 maichon main aath ank lekar sabase neeche rahi
 This is the first time in the history of IPL when the Dhoni-led team is out before the play-offs in the tournament
 punjab kii shuruuaat dhimi lekin thos rahi or hashim amala (30) tathaa murali vijay (59) ne pehle wicket ke liye 60 ran jode
 Off-spinner r Ashwin, who took four wickets for Pune, broke the partnership by sending Amla to the pavilion, whose catch was caught by George Bailey
 score main paanch ran jude the ki wicketiper ridhimaan saaha (3) ko duusare spinner adam jampa ne out kiya
 After this, Vijay and Gurkeerat Singh shared a 58-run partnership to return the team to a good score
 vijay ne 41 gend main chaar chaukon or teen chhakkon kii madad se 59 ran banaae, jabaki gurkirat ne 30 gend main 51 ran banaae, jisamen teen chakke or teen chauke shaamil the
 The comments vijay ko 16wein over main aswin ne bold kiya, jabaki gurkirat 18wein over main unka aglaa shikaar bane
 Due to this, the run rate of Punjab was curbed and at one time the team looking towards 200 runs could score 172 runs for seven wickets
 puchhlle ballebaaj koi kamaal nahin kar paae
 In reply Pune did not start well and half of their team had returned to the pavilion in the 14th over when only 86 runs were left on the score board
 ajinkya rahane (19) or osman khwaja (30) acchhee shuruuaat dene main naakaam rahe
 George Bailey was dismissed for just nine runs, while Saurabh Tiwary scored 17 runs
 irfan pathan bhi tik nahin sake or do ran banaakar apana wicket ganvaa baithe
